 The Delhi High Court today dismissed their petitions challenging Congress's Rajya Sabha members Ambika Soni and Kumari Selja challenging government orders to vacate large bungalows located in Lutyens' Delhi, saying they tried to politicize the case
 nyaayamurti rajeev sahay andla ne 2014 ke aam chunaavon ke baad congress ke satta main nahin lautne kii sambhaavna ke bich party kii rajyasabha sadasyon ko bangalon ke aavanton ko hi sandigdh bataaya
 He said that he was saddened to learn that the two mps have tried to give political color to the matter merely to occupy a house which they are not entitled to
 nyaayadhish ne kaha, 'mujhe sampada nideshaalay dioi kii karrwai galat najar nahin aa rahi
 As already stated, it has been proved that in the capacity of former Union Ministers and now Rajya Sabha members, the petitioners are entitled to reside in type-seven accommodation and not in type-viii
 ' He said, 'despite this, the petitioners, at the time when the general elections of Lok Sabha, 2014 were being held, allotted accommodation for themselves beyond their rights
 ' nyaayadhish ne donon par 25-25 hajaar rupee kaa jurmaana lagaate hue kaha, 'main yah kehane ke liye vivash hum ki jab ki yachikakartaon kii raajnneetik party ke sattarudh dal banane kii sambhaavna khatm ho raheen thim, is str par unhen prime awaason kaa aavanton atyant sandigdh he
 ' adaalat ne yah bhi kaha ki yadi donon saansadon ko lagata tha ki ve in awaason kii hakdaar hai to bhi unhen apana daawa karne ke liye nayi sarkaar ke satta main aane kaa intjaar karnaa chahie tha

 khel mantri ajay maakan ne kaha ki agar antarrashtriya olympic samiti dou chemical ko landan olympic khelon ke praayojakon kii suchi se hataane se inkaar kar detii he to bharat in khelon kaa bahishkaar karegaa yaa nahin yah faisla karne main khilaadiyon kii bhoomika ahm hogi
 Maken said that he does not want to create any confusion in the minds of the players and hence the decision to boycott or not to play these games will be taken at the appropriate time
 khel mantri ne ek tivi kaarykram main kaha, ‘khilaadiyon ke dimag main koi bhram nahin he
 If we start consulting players, will we not create confusion
 isamen khilaadiyon kii bhoomika kaaphi ahm he
 ' unhone kaha, ‘khilaadi kya mahasoos karte hai, isaki hamaare faisle main ahm bhoomika hogi
 The decision we make will have an impact on it
 ’ yah poochne par ki tab sarkaar kya karegi agar iosi antat: dou chemical ko praayojakon kii suchi se hataane se inkaar kar degaa, maakan ne kaha, ‘yah mushkil sawaal he, bilkul kaalpanik
 We have not decided on it yet
 ’ He said, 'we have a plan but why disclose the plan right now
 ’ maakan ne jor dekar kaha ki sarkaar ne abhi faisla nahin kiya he ki bhartiya adhikari khelon ke udghaatan or samaapan samaaroh kaa bahishkaar karenge yaa nahin
 He said, 'we have not decided on it yet
 main is bare main kuch nahin kah saktaa
 We will keep in mind the feelings of the people of Bhopal as well as the players on this issue
 ’ khel mantri ne kaha, ‘ham in donon main se ek kaa chayan nahin karnaa chaahate
 As far as preparations are concerned, our preparations are going on in full swing
 hamane training ke liye sarvshereshth kochon or sarvshereshth jagahon ko chunaa he
 Asked if India would boycott the Games, Maken said, "I don't want to say anything about it
" mujhe ab bhi ummid he ki ham samaadhaan dhundne main safal rahenge
 Maken said that if the Dow was not removed as a sponsor, it would mean that the Olympics had not gone spirit
 tippaniyan He said, 'if you look at the Olympic Charter, he has laid down the seven fundamental principles of the Olympics and the first principle states that respect for global fundamental moral principles
 ’ unhone kaha, ‘unki (iosi) kii gatividhiyon ke chah varg hai or isamen se ek khel or paryaavaran he
 They are joining a company that bought Union Carbide and i don't think they can ethically claim sponsorship of a competition
 ’ Maken refused to change his stand even when it was told that an agreement had been reached on the matter in the Supreme Court and the Government of India had also agreed to it
 unhone kaha, ‘yah naitik jimmedaari he
 i am not going on the legal side of this
 jab ve naitikta kii baat karte hai to kya union carbide ne jo bhi galat chijen kii uske liye uski uttaradhikari company ko bhugtan nahin karnaa chahie
 Maken said, "is this (case) not before the Dobra Supreme Court?" sarkaar ke liye yah ab bhi vivaad he
 Why do you go to the legal side of it? ham olympic bhaavana ke tahat iosi se kah rahe hai ki vah us company ke saath nahin jude jiske peeche union carbide kaa itihaas he
 ' maakan ne kaha ki vah khilaadiyon ke dimag main koi bhram paidaa nahin karnaa chaahate or isliye in khelon kaa bahishkaar karne yaa nahin karne kaa faisla uchit samay aane par kiya jayega
 The Sports Minister said in a TV program, 'there is no confusion in the minds of the players
 agar ham khilaadiyon se salaah mashvira shuru kar den to kya ham bhram paidaa nahin karenge
 The role of the players is very important in this
 ’ He said, 'what the players feel, it will play an important role in our decision
 ham jo faisla karte hai us par iskaa asar padegaa
 Asked what the government would do if the IOC eventually refuses to remove Dow Chemical from its list of sponsors, Maken said, "this is a difficult question, absolutely hypothetical
" hamane ab tak is par faisla nahin kiya he
 ' unhone kaha, ‘hamaare paas yojana he lekin abhi yojana kaa khulaasa kyon karen
 Maken insisted that the government had not yet decided whether Indian officials would boycott the opening and closing ceremonies of the Games
 unhone kaha, ‘hamane ab tak is par faisla nahin kiya he
 i cannot say anything about this
 ham is mudde par bhopal ke logon or saath hi khilaadiyon kii bhaawanaaon ko bhi dhyaan main rakhenge
 The Sports Minister said, "we do not want to choose one of these two
" jahaan tak taiyaariyon kaa sawaal he to hamaari taiyaariyaan joro par chal rahi hai
 We have chosen the best coaches and best places to train
 ’ yah poochne par ki kya bharat khelon kaa bahishkaar karegaa, maakan ne kaha, ‘main is bare main kuch nahin kahana chahta
 i still hope that we will be able to find a solution
 ’ maakan ne kaha ki agar dou ko praayojak ke rup main nahin hataaya gaya to iskaa matlab hoga ki olympic bhaavana par nahin chalaa gaya
 The comments unhone kaha, ‘agar aap olympic charter ko dekho to unhone olympic ke saat moolbhoot siddhant rakhe hai or pehle siddhant main kaha gaya he ki vaishvik moolbhoot naitik siddhanton kaa sammaan
 He said, 'he (IOC) has six classes of activities and one of them is sports and environment
 ve ek aisi company se jud rahe hai jisane union carbide ko kharida or mujhe nahin lagata he ki vah naitik rup se kisi pratiyogita ke praayojan kaa daawa kar sakate hai
 ' jab yah bataaya gaya ki ucchtam nyaayalay main is maamle par samjhauta ho gaya he or bharat sarkaar bhi isse sahamat ho gai thi to bhi maakan ne apana rukh badalane se inkaar kar diya
 He said, 'it is a moral responsibility
 main iske kanoonee paksh par nahin ja rahaa
